C[StdMeshers_QuadraticMesh](d5/dee/classStdMeshers__QuadraticMesh.html)|
Hypothesis for
[StdMeshers_Regular_1D](df/d00/classStdMeshers__Regular__1D.html), forcing
construction of quadratic edges. If the 2D mesher sees that all boundary edges
are quadratic ones, it generates quadratic faces, else it generates linear
faces using medium nodes as if they were vertex ones. The 3D mesher generates
quadratic volumes only if all boundary faces are quadratic ones, else it fails
